 ```python
# Simulating the chess game environment
class ChessGame:
    def __init__(self):
        self.board = [
            ['r', 'n', 'b', 'q', 'k', 'b', 'n', 'r'],
            ['p', 'p', 'p', 'p', 'p', 'p', 'p', 'p'],
            [' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' '],
            [' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' '],
            [' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' '],
            [' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' ', ' '],
            ['P', 'P', 'P', 'P', 'P', 'P', 'P', 'P'],
            ['R', 'N', 'B', 'Q', 'K', 'B', 'N', 'R']
        ]

    def get_current_board(self):
        return self.board

    def get_legal_moves(self):
        # For simplicity, let's assume all pieces can move like a king (one square in any direction)
        legal_moves = []
        for i in range(8):
            for j in range(8):
                if self.board[i][j] != ' ':
                    # Check up
                    if i > 0 and self.board[i-1][j] == ' ':
                        legal_moves.append(f'{chr(97+j)}{8-i}{8-(i-1)}')
                    # Check down
                    if i < 7 and self.board[i+1][j] == ' ':
                        legal_moves.append(f'{chr(97+j)}{8-i}{8+(i+1)}')
                    # Check left
                    if j > 0 and self.board[i][j-1] == ' ':
                        legal_moves.append(f'{chr(97+j)}{8-i}{chr(97+j-1)}')
                    # Check right
                    if j < 7 and self.board[i][j+1] == ' ':
                        legal_moves.append(f'{chr(97+j)}{8-i}{chr(97+j+1)}')
        return legal_moves

# Initialize the game
game = ChessGame()

# Get current board status
current_board = game.get_current_board()
print("Current Board Status:")
for row in current_board:
    print(' '.join(row))
print()

# Get legal moves for black
legal_moves = game.get_legal_moves()
print("Legal Moves (UCI format):", legal_moves)
```
